Thus, in the Kharkiv region, 145 hazards, 21.33 ha of forest areas, almost 171 km of line -electric programs, 40 km of gas pipelines, 192 km of roads, 239 000 sq.mq. different buildings. 6 044 GNP was disposed of and destroyed.

The sappers of the Armed Forces of the Armed Forces also operate in the territory of the communities of Kherson region, which are redeemed from occupation. More than 1189 casage land was cleared from GNP, almost 78 square meters of buildings, 5 facilities were checked. 4 095 GNP was damaged and destroyed.

The White Angel group evacuates people from Avdiivka, who is in the Red Zone

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-04-02T58:00:00-04:00

Description: About Chester, National Police. Evakuacіina Grupa "Bili Yangol" to Vykhvykanz ... War with Ukraine 2022, War with Ukraine Latest News today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last for today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia and when the war with Ukraine will be either in 2022 No, will there be a war with Ukraine in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukrainian news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['642805df04ed4211768041.jpg', '642805cb051c4568278921.jpg', '642805d49bcca427716354.jpg', '642805d49ac38245462836.jpg', '642805daa07a1472567930.jpg']

Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АВДІЇВКА', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'БІЛИЙ ЯНГОЛ', 'ВІЙНА', 'ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'НАЦПОЛІЦІЯ']

Category: News

About it reportsNational Police.

The White Angel Evacuation Group exports residents on armored cops. To help everyone quickly respond to shelling, police formed additional products.

Evacuation occurs under the coordination of Donetsk ova, also involved in the SES rescuers. About 1900 residents remain in Avdiivka. Most of them live in the private sector in the old part of the city. In addition to the White Angels, the Red Zone is directed by police detachments. The task of law enforcement officers is instant assistance to the population during air strikes and artillery attacks, the number of which has increased significantly.

Avdiivka streets are extinct. People come out of shelters only for food, water. But every way out is a deadly risk. “Recently, the woman died when she went to the well to collect water. The man was injured, ”says Gennady Yudin, a member of the White Angel crew.

To travel to the right address, the police officer is forced to first clear the road from pieces of concrete and plastic - what was previously a house. Gennady's shells and fragments carefully go around. In an armored car - coal wheels, medical tools, children's bulletproof vests. Everything that may be needed for salvation.

This time, the police evacuated the elderly, who were asked to take away their natives who left earlier. One of the inhabitants first planted the cat on the cat by the Taadvorov Dog Aleska, for which he looked after and took with him to a safe place. It was very scary, ” - says another passenger.

Both "white angels" - locals and understand the residents, because their families also experience the same. "My grandmother lived here on the fifth floor," shows Dmitry Solovaya, the Believed House "White Angel".

Police traveled locations where people can be extinguished. In addition, the route checked the property in broken stores where masters can operate. After the missile strike, the angels were found on the ground a shabby, Alevtsy Flag and returned it to the place of fluttering as a symbol of unbroken Avdiivka.While this material was being prepared, a tragedy occurred in Avdiivka-a 5-month-old baby and his grandmother were fired. Parents are hospitalized with injuries. The back before the arrival, the police persuaded their mother to leave and save the baby. Tsebula is not the first attempt to convince the woman, but in vain. The enemy is chaotic of life -long houses, so the only way to survive is to evacuate until it is too late.

Category: News

Twitter has blocked the US expert Scott Ritter, who actively distinguished Russian propaganda of narratives.

About it reportsThe Center for Combating Misinformation on your Facebook page.

According to Twitter's official policy, the platform blocks accounts that violate the rules of safety, confidentiality and authenticity.

Ritter was outraged by the Twitter decision, calling such actions an attempt to force him.

“Today I have the courage to challenge the US government against its surrounding policy in Ukraine. And instead of attracting me to debate, dialogue and discussions, they try to make me silent by closing myacaunt on Twitter, ”he said.

This is not the first time the platform blocks the expert's account. About a year ago, the Twitter closed Ritter's account after he published a post in which US President Joe Baiden "a military criminal" and unrighteoused that the National Police of Ukraine was responsible for atrocities in Bucha.

“The enemy TG channels spread a fake, the basis of which became several photos of the Armed Forces of the Armed Forces with a tag" not for sale "in one of the Turkish classical clothing stores.

We warn!

Do not trust the materials that appeal to emotions, because excessive emotionality precipitates critical thinking and helps the perception of hostile fakes. "

За словами глави NASA, разом уся команда проєкту Artemis II відкриває нову ерудосліджень для нового покоління «зоряних мрійників».

Очікується, що політ експедиції триватиме близько десяти днів, та матиме наметі перевірку систем життєзабезпечення космічного корабля Orion, а такожможливості для життя й роботи в далекому космосі.

Registration for a national multi -compartment test on the test portal of the Ukrainian Education Quality Assessment Center will be available for graduates of the year and those entrants who want to improve the possibilities and their results that they have received last years in order to submit in this way in order Again, documents to higher education institutions. Registration will be long -sided on April 3, May 3. This is very important, ”Vitrenko said.

Read also: He noted that this year there is a certain peculiarity in the preparation of NMT, which is chosen by the choice of the third subject.

“If all the subjects were binding last year, there are two obligatory subjects this year: Ukrainian language and literature and mathematics. And a third -subject - whether history or foreign language, physics, chemistry or biology will be entrants in their e -office must choose the subject of the subject, because the national multi -enthusiastic test will be personified and it will be for each entrant on the set registration, ”the Deputy Minister of Education Insuki emphasized.

Talking about the registration algorithm, he noted that then it is necessary to build copies of the identity documents and send to the checking of regional quality assessment centers.

Read also: “Within seven days, you have to answer the center. The answer can be or “you are registered for the delivery of a national multi -grade test” and in which center, which you will also choose when registering or “denied”. If you are referred, you will need to contact the regional centers or repeat the registration. Maybe not all the documents you have bored into your electronic office, ”the official explained.Vitrenko also noted that "this year every entrant can submit 5 declaring a budget form of study and up to 20 applications for a contract."

Medical rehabilitation of premature children is carried out in 128 hospitals - MOH

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-04-03T-57:32:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-04-03T21:32:00+03:00

Description: Rehabilitation for the first three years of life for infants who were born premature and/or patients is carried out at 128 hospitals of Ukraine. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_15858..."]

Tags: ['Діти', 'МОЗ', 'Реабілітація', 'Лікарня']

Type: Article

Rehabilitation during the first three years of life for babies, who were born in advance and/or patients, is carried out at 128 hospitals of Ukraine.

This is reported on , reports Ukrinform.

"Medical rehabilitation of children under three years of age, who were born prematurely and/abnormalities, is free of charge in all medical institutions of Ukraine, which have a contract with the NSAU. There are 128 hospitals all over the country. Most in Kyiv, Dnipropetrovsk and Lviv regions," - it reads message.

It is noted that such assistance is provided within the package of the Medical Care Program "Medical care for newborns in difficult neonatal cases". For those who need further rehabilitation, the package "Medical rehabilitation, which were born premature and/or sick during the first three years of life" is provided.

The MoH notes that parents can choose any hospital that has a contract of ZSZU in this direction, regardless of the place of registration . It is possible to obtain such a medical assistance with the regulation of the primary care physician with whom the declaration is concluded, with a statement of the attending physician, in case of transfer from another medical establishment of the hospital.

Read also: Within the package free of charge for patients-children are:

  • work of multidisciplinary rehabilitation team - from the primary examination and consultation of a specialist, making a rehabilitation diagnosis and forming an individual rehabilitation program for the provision of rehabilitation services; * laboratory and instrumental examinations; * Rehabilitation services regardless of the child's place of residence; * counseling of the child by doctors of other specialties in accordance with its condition; * special screening for the detection of autistic spectrum disorders; * nutrition of the child in the hospital; * Selection and adaptation of special equipment and alternative communication facilities for the child and more. Read also: Full that are included in the package available on the NSAU website in the "Requirements 2023"(paragraph 30 “Medical rehabilitation of infants who were born prematurely and/abysses during the first three years of life”).

Як повідомлялося, в Програмі медичних гарантій на 2023 рік передбачено 39пакетів медичних послуг. Бюджет ПМГ становить понад 142 млрд грн.

The center has a room for children aged 3 to 8 years, where children can leave children up to four hours a day. In addition to working people, the room for children also works on Saturday from 10 to 14 o'clock. The educators speak Ukrainian and Russian.

Preliminary registration at the Assistance Center available free consultations, which are also provided online. It is about psychologists for adults, young people, lawyers, midwives, specialists in stay legalization, business consultants, career consultants and more.

Information meetings with different experts are also cyclical, during which you can learn about different aspects of life in Poland, such as searching for work or a child's recording to school.

All services at the Polish Migration Forum Fund are provided free of charge. The center will help all foreigners, no matter when and where they went to Poland. Experts advise in different languages, including Ukrainian, Russian, Polish, Belarusian, English, French, Spanish, Chechen, Dari, Pushta.

Business has improved the prospects of its activity a little

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-04-03T15:45:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-04-03T15:45:00+03:00

Description: Enterprises of all sectors in March more optimistic evaluated the results and prospects of their activities. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16546..."]

Tags: ['Бізнес', 'Нацбанк']

Type: Article

Enterprises of all sectors in March more optimistic evaluated the results of their activities.

As Ukrinform reports, this is evidenced by a business activity index(IODA), which National Bank calculates on a monthly basis, reports .

"Improvement of external conditions, logistics, situation in , increasing consumer moms have a positive impact on the expectations of business in March, " - said the news.

In March 2023, the IODA increased to 49.5 out of 45.0 in February and almost reach. This is the highest value since December 2021.

Trade companies provided the most optimistic estimates of the results of their activities against the background of consumer mood revival, improvement of energy supply and increased supply of goods: Sectoral Index increased to 53.6 from 47.0 in February, crossing the neutral level for the first time after November 2021. Respondents have significantly improved their turnover on turnover and the volume of purchase of goods for sale.

Read also: Improvement of the situation in energy and external conditions, as well as adjusting the supply chains have positively affected the estimates of the respondentity. For the first time after February 2022, they expected an increase in their economic results compared to the previous month: the sectoral index crossed the neutral level and amounted to 51.2 compared to 47.2 Ulita. Respondents expected an increase in the volume of manufactured products and new products for products, including export. At the same time, pessimism has declined in estimates of work in progress(unfulfilled orders)But the expectations of growth of residual products have weakened.In spite of the seasonal revival, the services of the service sector had the most rapid estimates about their economic prospects: the sectoral index was 45.7 comparable to 43.2 in February. The respondents were somewhat mitigated, but have maintained negative awareness of the volume of services provided, new orders, as well as volume services in the process of execution.

Most enterprises involved in the survey predict the slowdown in the growth rate of purchase prices and prices of contractors, as well as values and tariffs for their own products or services.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-04-03T19:26:12+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-04-03T19:26:12+03:00

Description: For the first time in the last 59 years, the PRC has changed the position on the issue of the Kuril Islands, and now Beijing occupies a "neutral" position. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_15653..."]

Tags: ['Японія', 'Китай', 'Курильські острови', 'росія']

Type: Article

For the first time in the last 59 years, the PRC has changed the position on the issue of belonging of the Kuril islands, now Beijing occupies a "neutral" position.

As Ukrinform reports, it reports .

The news agency, with reference to the words of its own source, notes that the head of Japan did not support Japan's claim on the captured by the occupied Russia near Hokkaido during negotiations with the President of the Russian Federation Vladimirputin last month, abandoning the ancient position of their recognition.

During the meetings in Moscow, Putin said that China "did not support any scene" in this territorial dispute, moving to the policy of the neutrality of China's position, formed by the then Chinese leader of Mao Zedong in 1964, considering four disputed islands as the territory of Japan.

Read also: Bilateral negotiations on islands known as northern territories in Japan and southern smoking in Russia were suspended after Tokyo imposed on Moscow after its invasion of Ukraine.

Change of position It can complicate the dispute that lasts for decades, since Moscow is unlikely to have been in this matter now, with Beijing's support, viewers believe.

In July 1964, Mao Zedong told a delegation of the Socialist Party of Japan, who arrived on a visit to China, which was captured by Russia, "Need to return", that is, announced the support of Tokyo territorial claims by Beijing.

The Chinese government has taken this position, although in recent years it has been publicly not aware of it. On the maps made in China, the controversial islands are marked as "occupied by Russia."

Read also: Japan claims to the South Kuril Islands according to the Protective Treatment and the Borders of 1855. In Japan, a territorial dispute with the Russian Federation is officially the issues of "northern territories". At the same time, Russia insists that the smokers were part of the USSR in the Second World War.

It is about insulation of facades, roofs, basements, installation of energy efficient windows and front doors, meters and system control of energy consumption, modernization of heating systems, ventilation and more.

The final beneficiaries of the program are local governments. It will be selected from April 3 to June 3, 2023 inclusive. Questions about the selection of thermo -modernization and requests for clarification can be sent to upbee.support@mtu.gov.ua by 3 June 2023.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Modified Time: 2023-04-03T21:32:00+03:00

Description: Rehabilitation for the first three years of life for infants who were born premature and/or patients is carried out at 128 hospitals of Ukraine. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_15858..."]

Tags: ['Діти', 'МОЗ', 'Реабілітація', 'Лікарня']

Type: Article

Rehabilitation during the first three years of life for babies, who were born in advance and/or patients, is carried out at 128 hospitals of Ukraine.

This is reported on , reports Ukrinform.

"Medical rehabilitation of children under three years of age, who were born prematurely and/abnormalities, is free of charge in all medical institutions of Ukraine, which have a contract with the NSAU. There are 128 hospitals all over the country. Most in Kyiv, Dnipropetrovsk and Lviv regions," - it reads message.

It is noted that such assistance is provided within the package of the Medical Care Program "Medical care for newborns in difficult neonatal cases". For those who need further rehabilitation, the package "Medical rehabilitation, which were born premature and/or sick during the first three years of life" is provided.

The MoH notes that parents can choose any hospital that has a contract of ZSZU in this direction, regardless of the place of registration . It is possible to obtain such a medical assistance with the regulation of the primary care physician with whom the declaration is concluded, with a statement of the attending physician, in case of transfer from another medical establishment of the hospital.

Read also: Within the package free of charge for patients-children are:

  • work of multidisciplinary rehabilitation team - from the primary examination and consultation of a specialist, making a rehabilitation diagnosis and forming an individual rehabilitation program for the provision of rehabilitation services; * laboratory and instrumental examinations; * Rehabilitation services regardless of the child's place of residence; * counseling of the child by doctors of other specialties in accordance with its condition; * special screening for the detection of autistic spectrum disorders; * nutrition of the child in the hospital; * Selection and adaptation of special equipment and alternative communication facilities for the child and more. Read also: Full that are included in the package available on the NSAU website in the "Requirements 2023"(paragraph 30 “Medical rehabilitation of infants who were born prematurely and/abysses during the first three years of life”).

Як повідомлялося, в Програмі медичних гарантій на 2023 рік передбачено 39пакетів медичних послуг. Бюджет ПМГ становить понад 142 млрд грн.

About it reports Ukrinform with reference to .

Images: ['free-legal-aid442-3.jpg']

Tags: ['МІНРЕІНТЕГРАЦІЇ', 'СОЦЗАХИСТ ПІД ЧАС ВІЙНИ']

Category: News

Illustrative photo

All released from hostile captivity and families of persons illegally devoid of freedom Federation are entitled to primary legal assistance. In particular, entry legal advice, assistance in writing applications or complaints.

About it reportsMinistry of Inquiries of Reintegration of Temporarily Occupied Territories of Ukraine.

If the commission in the Ministry of reintegration establishes the fact of deprivation of these persons as a result of armed aggression against Ukraine, they can receive free legal assistance for free. The Denmark Ministry has concluded an agreement with Norway to jointly transfer thousand artillery shells.

About it reportsThe press service of the Danish defense department.

Thanks to the new Danish-Norwegian cooperation, Denmark will further increase its military contribution to Ukraine.

“Ukrainians continue to have a great and urgent need for ammunition to combat Russia. Together with other EU and NATO countries, Denmark prepares various help. Our cooperation with Norway is an important example of this, ”said Acting. Denmark's Defense Minister Troels Lund Polesen.

Cooperation of countries means that the Danish industry will collect the corps of the Norwegian 155mm artillery shells with compatible Danish metal charges, arresters and inflammatory pipes in full artillery shells. The afternoons are transferred to the defense of Ukraine.

“Ukraine is in need of artillery ammunition, and we can help. For the safety of Europe and Norway, it is important that Ukraine manages to defend the attack of Russia, ”Norwegian Defense Minister Bjorn Arildgrams emphasized.

The Denmark Ministry of Defense believes that ammunition will be able to use the Danish artillery settings of Caesar, which Denmark's parliament has decided to transfer to Ukraine the beginning of the year.

Russia's unjustified and unjustified military aggression against Ukraine is destroyed by the security system in the Black Sea-Azov region. In order to find an effective toolingary to answer these challenges and to provide the possibility of sustainable development to all peaceful countries of the region, Ukraine initiated the first Black Sea Security Conference to be held in conjunction with Romania on April 12-13.

The event will be held within the framework of the International Crimean Platform - Mechanism, aimed at de -occupation of Crimea, restoration of the Black Sea, European and Global Security.

Organizers of the Conference: Ministry of Foreign Affairs of Ukraine, Ministry of Defense of Ukraine, Ministry of Foreign Affairs of Romania, Ministry of State Defense of Romania, in partnership with the Center for Defense Strategies(Ukraine).

У центрі уваги також будуть питання інформаційної війни та кібератак.

Програма конференції

_Перший день (expert): _

  • Presentation of the study "Future Security Configuration of the Black and Azov Seas" from the expert network of the Crimean platform, expert discussion.

  • Expert discussion "First Cyberwar".

  • Expert discussion "How the Russian Information War is underway and why it challenges the international security system."

_Second day(Official representatives): _

  • Panel discussion "Lessons obtained: full -scale invasion of the Russian Federation into Ukraine, its multidimensional influence and lessons for the democratic world."

  • Panel discussion "Plan for today: immediate response to current threats and challenges in the Black Sea region".

  • Panel discussion "Future Configuration: What is the future of regional security in the Black and Azov Seas? On the way to the Euro -Atlantic strategy for a stable, safe and prosperous region. "

An indictment was sent to court with respect to a serviceman of the armed Sylrf, who was abused by Irpen residents and imitated their execution.

About it reportsOffice of the Prosecutor General of Ukraine.

The investigation found that during March 2022, the Senior Streach Staff of the 104th Guards Airborne Assault Red Labor Regiment, together with other Russian servicemen, conducted special raids in Irpin.

“They are cruelly, abusive and humiliating with the civilian population, trying to identify patriotic citizens of Ukraine. In the territory of the Irpin military hospital, they found two civilians. The interrogative, but not receiving the desired information, the accused ordered the men of the Belin Kolin and lean their heads to each other. In order to intimidate, he imitated their shooting, making several shots over the heads of men, ”the message goes.

Subsequently, he, together with other military personnel of the Russian Federation, illegally penetrated a life house where there were two civilians.

“They struck the torso and the head of the victim and, imitating the murder, fired his head. There, the military of the Russian Federation allegedly due to the failure to provide "truthful information", sent automatic weapons to the victim, "the Prosecutor General's office was assigned.

The accused is now in custody.

Category: News

Today, on April 3, the General Fund of the State Budget of Ukraine a first tranche of $ 2.7 billion. USA(2 billion SDR)from the International Bulk Fund(IMF). Про цеповідомляєGovernment portal.

Funds received under the new four -year expanded funding program(Extended Fund Facility — EFF)For Ukraine, which is $ 15.6 billion. USA(11.6 billion SDR).

«Сьогодні Україна отримала перший транш за новою програмою від МВФ. Завдякинаданим коштам ми спроможні й надалі зберігати економічну стабільність вУкраїні, а також забезпечувати пріоритетні видатки державного бюджету», —зазначив Міністр фінансів України Сергій Марченко.

Довідково

У п’ятницю, 31 березня, Рада директорів МВФ затвердила нову чотирирічнупрограму розширеного фінансування (Extended Fund Facility — EFF)For Ukraine, finance of $ 15.6 billion. USA(11.6 billion SDR).

Програма включає два етапи. На першому етапі, що запланований на 2023-24 роки,увага зосереджена на впровадженні надійного бюджету на 2023 рік та збільшеннімобілізації доходів, у тому числі шляхом уникнення заходів, які можутьзменшити податкові надходження. Під час першого етапу також передбачаєтьсязниження інфляції та утримання обмінного курсу, в тому числі за допомогоюпідтримки відповідних валютних резервів. Крім того, очікуються заходи щодосприяння довгостроковій фінансовій стабільності, включно з підготовкою більшглибокої оцінки стану банківського сектору, а також продовженням сприяннянезалежності НБУ.

Під час другого етапу програми буде зроблено фокус на реформах, які допоможутьмаксимально ефективно підтримувати післявоєнне відновлення та реконструкцію, атакож допоможуть Україні імплементувати необхідні заходи на шляху доєвроінтеграції. Довгострокове зростання економіки також є одним з пріоритетівдругого етапу програми EFF.

The US Administration categorically rejects any Russian Vlad's allegations to the journalist The Wall Street Journal Evan Gershkovich in the kind of assassination of spying.

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-04-04T99:00:00-04:00

Images: ['whatsapp-image-2022-02-22-at-16.12.00.jpeg']

Tags: ['ДОПОМОГА ВЕТЕРАНАМ', 'ЦНАП', 'ЮЛІЯ ЛАПУТІНА']

Category: News

Provision of quality services to war veterans and their families through networking network provision of administrative services(CNAP)It will be an effective instrument to declare Ukrainian defenders and defenders and their families to a peaceful life, and will promote decent self -realization in society. This was stressed by the Minister of Executive of Veterans of Ukraine Yulia Laputina during an online meeting with the heads of the tsar, which took place on April 3 with the assistance of the All-Ukrainian Association of Administrative Services, [reports] reportsGovernment portal.

The head of the Ministry of Justice noted that providing a proper and quality service to members of their families and families of the fallen is one of the main tasks defined by the government within the framework of the formation of complex veteran policy. For this Ministry of Veterans, a series of teachings of the CNAP administrators of all the houses of Ukraine has already begun.

The students will get acquainted with the list of veterans services, practical cases of interaction with veterans and veterans in CNAPs, will receive answers to the most common issues from specialists of profile units of mineveterans and psychologists.

“One of the important directions of our partnership is the expansion of the list of lists of services provided to veterans of war through CNAPs. The Ministry of Justice has prepared a draft order of the Government, which will add 19 new services for veterans, the provision of which is provided by CNAPs. These are, in particular, services for cash assistance or compensation, free of charge, replacement of UBD certificates and members of the families of defenders and defenders, etc., ”Yulia Laputina reported.

In addition, the Ministry of Veterans already implement separate partnership projects jointly by the content authorities. In particular, Zhytomyr's territorial community is already working successfully. There, on the basis of the CNAP, a "uniform" for veterans was opened, and employees who were trained in guarantees, rights and opportunities for veterans, are involved in his work.

And together with the local authorities of the city of the Dnieper, it is planned to implement the project "I - Vetran", in the future of which - the introduction of 112 of the most sought after service of the city.She told the participants of the meeting created by specialists of the Ministry on the basis of the State Register of War Veterans Portal "E-Vetran"-to inform and the provision of qualified services to Ukrainian veterans, members of their families and families of fallen soldiers.

“CNAP experts provide a large list of administrative services to different persons. And those social instruments that are in the centers will become a cooperation with Ministry of Veterans. We must be prepared for the massive return of Ukrainian soldiers after victory, to promote their qualitative zesting reintegration to families, our communities. And the human -centric approach of providing services will strengthen social unity and add a stable state. I thank everyone for their readiness to cooperate with the Ministry of Veterans, together we will make a very useful business, ”Yulia Laputina emphasized.
